Dear colleagues and students of the University!
We would like to inform you that due to the library stock increase, all the books were displaced to the open space of the Reading hall on the 3rd floor at the University building.
Please note that you can get books or give them back according to the current library work schedule on Monday, Wednesday and Friday from 13:00 till 17:30.
We kindly ask you not to cross safety barrier and not to take books from the shelves after working hours.

Please be aware that we carry out video surveillance in order to ensure safety of the library stock.

Best regards,
Innopolis University Team
